Beginner's Basics

Show/hide all levels
Active Irena's Wind Piercing
Master Level 5
Description Summons Irena to inflicts significant damage to multiple monsters with a single powerful blow. Skill level can be increased depending on your level.
Level 1 MP Cost: 15, Damage: 530%, Max Enemies Penetrated: 4
5 MP Cost: 27, Damage: 750%, Max Enemies Penetrated: 6

Master Level 5
Description Summons Irena to inflicts significant damage to multiple monsters with a single powerful blow. Skill level can be increased depending on your level.

Show/hide all levels
Active Irena's Wind
Master Level 10
Description Summons a spirit that automatically performs an area attack on the enemies you are fighting. Skill level increases by 1 every 15 levels.
Level 1 MP Cost: 11, Damage: 70%, Duration: 110 sec
The damage of Ultimate Explorer minion skills is calculated differently from that of the character.
10 MP Cost: 20, Damage: 160%, Duration: 200 sec
The damage of Ultimate Explorer minion skills is calculated differently from that of the character.

Show/hide all levels
Passive Adventurer's Curiosity
Master Level 6
Description Your curiosity and attention to detail grants you bonuses to Critical Rate and the chance of adding monsters to your Monster Collection.
This bonus is multiplicative rather than additive.
This Link Skill can be stacked up to 3 times, once for each unique Explorer Bowman job character you have on this world.
Level 1 Chance to add monsters to Monster Collection: +10%, Critical Rate: +3%
6 Chance to add monsters to Monster Collection: +35%, Critical Rate: +10%
Passive Adventurer's Curiosity
Master Level 6
Description Your curiosity and attention to detail grants you bonuses to Critical Rate and the chance of adding monsters to your Monster Collection.
This bonus is multiplicative rather than additive.
This Link Skill can be stacked up to 3 times, once for each unique Explorer Bowman job character you have on this world.

Active Return to Partem
Master Level 1
Description Return to Karuppa Town.
Level 1 Returns you to Karuppa Town when used.
Cooldown 600 sec


Passive Ancient Curse
Master Level 1
Description Many of your stats are reduced by the influence of an unknown curse.
As a result, you can only equip the exclusive Ancient Bow weapon, but the effect of the curse weakens as the equipped relic grows stronger.
Skills using the Ancient Bow do not consume arrows separately.
Level 1

The Archer's Art

Passive Curse Dampening I
Master Level 1
Description Releases power built up in the relic through continuous combat to weaken the effects of the Ancient Curse.
Level 1 Activated when attacking with a Cardinal Force skill. Accumulates up to level 10, with a Critical Rate increase of 2% for each level.
Can only be activated when the curse is reducing your Critical Rate.
Show/hide all levels
Active Cardinal Deluge
Master Level 20
Description [Cardinal Force]
An archery technique that zeroes in on targets within range. Guided shots target the boss with the highest Max HP first if there is a boss within range, and are unaffected by attack reflection.
Level 20 required to learn Cardinal Deluge Amplification.
Level 1 MP Cost: 5, Max Enemies Hit: 4. Blasts an arrow that deals 52% damage 4 times.
20 MP Cost: 10, Max Enemies Hit: 4. Blasts an arrow that deals 90% damage 4 times.

Active Double Jump
Master Level 10
Description Allows you to use the Double Jump skill to move very quickly. Double-tap the up arrow key to jump again while in mid-air. Double-tap the down arrow key to descend more quickly. If you use Action Customization, you can move up in the air with the up arrow and jump keys, and descend with the down arrow and jump keys.
Right-click to toggle Action Customization ON/OFF.
Level 1 MP Cost: 28, allows you to jump a greater distance
10 MP Cost: 10, allows you to jump a greater distance

Master Level 15

The Ancient Power and the Dark Curse

Passive Relic Charge I
Master Level 1
Description Gathers energy in the relic through combat. The use of a Cardinal Force skill will cause the relic's emblem to shift, and a successful hit will add to the gauge.
Using Ancient Force skills will consume the built-up gauge. After using a Cardinal Force skill, you can chain other Cardinal Force or Ancient Force skills together, allowing them to be used more quickly.
Level 1 Relic Gauge Maximum Charge: 1000
Attacking an enemy with a Cardinal Force skill charges the relic gauge by 10, and by 5 for every guided arrow of Cardinal Deluge that hits an enemy.
If a different Cardinal Force skill is used next, the cooldown for all Ancient Force skills will be reduced by 0.5, except for the 5th Job Advancement skills.


Passive Curse Dampening II
Master Level 1
Description Releases power built up in the relic through continuous combat to further weaken the effects of the Ancient Curse.
Level 1 Activated when attacking with a Cardinal Force skill. Accumulates up to level 10, with a Defense increase of 2% for each level.
Can only be activated when the curse is reducing your Defense.
Show/hide all levels
Passive Cardinal Deluge Amplification
Master Level 10
Description [Cardinal Force]
Enhances the Cardinal Deluge skill.
Level 10 required to learn Advanced Cardinal Force
Level 1 MP Cost: 10. Fires an arrow that deals 110% damage to up to 5 enemies 4 times.
If a boss is within the attack's range, fires 1 additional arrows. The additional arrows target the boss with the highest HP first.
10 MP Cost: 15. Fires an arrow that deals 200% damage to up to 5 enemies 4 times.
If a boss is within the attack's range, fires 1 additional arrows. The additional arrows target the boss with the highest HP first.

Active Cardinal Burst
Master Level 20
Description [Cardinal Force]
An archery technique that launches an explosive arrow of condensed energy that flies straight ahead. The arrow will detonate when it hits an enemy or reaches its maximum range.
Level 20 required to learn Cardinal Burst Boost.
Level 1 MP Cost: 10, Max Enemies: 5, Damage: 105%, Attack Count: 4, when the arrow explodes.
20 MP Cost: 15, Max Enemies: 5, Damage: 200%, Attack Count: 4, when the arrow explodes.

Active Swarm Shot
Master Level 19
Description [Ancient Force]
Call on the relic's power to imbue a shot with a mysterious aura. Each time the arrow pierces an enemy, additional magic arrows will split off and attack nearby enemies.
Level 1 Relic Gauge Cost: 50, Max Enemies Hit: 8, Damage: 110%, Attack Count: 4. Creates 2 magical arrows that deal 55% damage 4 times each time this attack pierces an enemy.
Cooldown: 10 sec.
19 Relic Gauge Cost: 50, Max Enemies Hit: 8, Damage: 200%, Attack Count: 4. Creates 2 magical arrows that deal 100% damage 4 times each time this attack pierces an enemy.
Cooldown: 10 sec.

Passive Bountiful Deluge
Master Level 20
Description Manifest the power stored within the relic to call forth magical arrows that chase and attack enemies in range for a set time.
These magical arrows target the boss with the highest Max HP first, and are not affected by attack reflection.
Required skill: Cardinal Deluge Amplification Lv. 5
Level 1 When using Cardinal Burst while the relic displays the Deluge emblem, there is a 2% chance to create 3 magical arrows.
These magical arrows will chase and attack nearby enemies for 2 sec, dealing 62% damage 3 times.
20 When using Cardinal Burst while the relic displays the Deluge emblem, there is a 40% chance to create 3 magical arrows.
These magical arrows will chase and attack nearby enemies for 2 sec, dealing 100% damage 3 times.

Active Cardinal Torrent
Master Level 20
Description [Cardinal Force]
An archery technique used to achieve high mobility. Release Swiftstrike Energy stored in your weapon as a short burst of speed that propels you to your destination, then swing your weapon to attack nearby enemies.
You can use the directional keys to move left, right, or up with this skill. If used without directional input, you will swing your weapon at your current location.
Level 20 required to learn Advanced Cardinal Force
Level 1 MP Cost: 15, Consumes 1 Swiftstrike Charge
Deals 305% damage 5 times to up to 6 nearby enemies.
You gain 1 Swiftstrike Charge every 7 sec, and can store up to a maximum of 5.
20 MP Cost: 20, Consumes 1 Swiftstrike Charge
Deals 400% damage 5 times to up to 6 nearby enemies.
You gain 1 Swiftstrike Charge every 7 sec, and can store up to a maximum of 5.

Passive Evasion Boost
Master Level 10
Description Chance to dodge enemy attacks. If you succeed, attacks you land in the next second will result in Critical Hits. Also increases Knockback Resistance permanently.
Level 1 Dodge Chance: 12%, all attacks following a successful dodge for 1 sec. will be critical hits, Knockback Resistance: +4%

Master of the Ancient Bow

Passive Relic Charge II
Master Level 1
Description With the relic finally made whole, its flow of energy has become more stable and potent, allowing you to enhance Enchant Force skills with the power of the Cardinal Force.
The currently-displayed emblem determines the characteristics of Enchant Force skills, and will be reset after an Enchant Force skill is used.
After using a Cardinal Force skill, you can chain Enchant Force skills to use them in quick succession.
Level 1 The Relic Gauge is charged by 20 when attacking an enemy with a Cardinal Force skill, and by 10 per hit from Cardinal Deluge's guided arrows.
The Shadow Raven will charge the Relic Gauge by 10 for each enemy hit by its attacks. When you use another Cardinal Force skill, all Ancient Force and Enchant Force skills will have their cooldowns reduced by 1 sec, except for 5th Job Advancement skills.


Passive Curseweaver
Master Level 1
Description Overcoming the Ancient Curse allows you to turn its debilitating effects on your foes in battle.
Bow skills will inflict the curse on enemies, and the Shadow Raven will focus its attention on enemies with the curse when summoned.
Level 1 Certain skills inflict Ancient Curse, which lasts for 30 sec and can be stacked up to 5 times.
Skills that use the Ancient Bow deal an additional 2% Critical Damage to enemies for each stack of the curse currently affecting them.


Active Curse Enchant Force
Master Level 1
Description The power of a certain curse can be inscribed on Enchant Force with the completed power of Relic.
Can be toggled On/Off.
Level 1 MP Cost: 80, Select a curse to inscribe on Enchant Force
Cooldown: 1 sec

Passive Bountiful Torrent
Master Level 20
Description Expands the power stored within the relic to hex your arrows with the curse's energy when using Deluge and Burst of Cardinal and Enchant skills. Permanently increases Attack Power.
Required Skill: Cardinal Torrent Lv. 20 or above
Level 1 When using Cardinal Force and Enchant Force skills with the Deluge or Burst emblems, your attack has a 2% chance to apply 1 stack of the Ancient Curse debuff.
Permanently increases your Attack Power by 1%.
20 When using Cardinal Force and Enchant Force skills with the Deluge or Burst emblems, your attack has a 40% chance to apply 1 stack of the Ancient Curse debuff.
Permanently increases your Attack Power by 20%.

Permanently increases your Attack Power by 21%.
22 When using Cardinal Force and Enchant Force skills with the Deluge or Burst emblems, your attack has a 44% chance to apply 1 stack of the Ancient Curse debuff.
Permanently increases your Attack Power by 22%.

Active Ancient Astra
Level Requirement 160
Master Level 1
Description [Enchant Force]
Manifest arrows like those spoken of in legend to rain destruction upon your foes.
Deluge Enhancement
Creates additional magical arrows when an enemy is hit.
Burst Enhancement
Take aim at an enemy and loose an arrow with maximum destructive power.
Torrent Enhancement
Grants the ability to attack while moving.
Level 1 Relic Gauge Cost: 65 per sec. Hold down the key to continuously attack up to 7 enemies, for 320% damage, 6 times.
This skill will end early if the Relic gauge doesn't have enough points.
Cooldown: 60 sec


Active Ancient Astra (Deluge)
Level Requirement 160
Master Level 1
Description [Enchant Force]
Manifest arrows like those spoken of in legend to rain destruction upon your foes.
Each enemy hit has a chance to generate additional magical arrows that attack nearby enemies. The magical arrows target the boss with the highest HP first.
Level 1 Relic Gauge Cost: 65 per sec. Hold down the key to continuously attack up to 7 enemies, for 400% damage, 6 times. Has a 30% chance to create 2 magical arrows that attack 2 times, dealing 240% damage.
While channeling this skill, damage taken from enemy attacks (including attacks that deal a fixed percentage of damage) is reduced by 60%.
This skill will end early if the Relic gauge doesn't have enough points.
Cooldown: 60 sec.


Active Ancient Astra (Burst)
Level Requirement 160
Master Level 1
Description [Enchant Force]
Manifest arrows like those spoken of in legend to rain destruction upon your foes.
Use the Up and Down arrow keys to control the firing angle. The arrow will detonate upon contact with the enemy or at the end of its range.
Level 1 Relic Gauge Cost: 65 per sec. Hold down the key to intermittently fire arrows at the designated angle. The arrows' explosions deal 1440% damage, 10 times, to up to 12 enemies. The first arrow fired with this skill cannot be angled and is fired straight ahead.
While channeling this skill, damage taken from enemy attacks (including attacks that deal a fixed percentage of damage) is reduced by 60%.
This skill will end early if the Relic gauge doesn't have enough points.
Cooldown: 60 sec.


Active Ancient Astra (Torrent)
Level Requirement 160
Master Level 1
Description [Enchant Force]
Manifest arrows like those spoken of in legend to rain destruction upon your foes.
Use the directional keys to move forward and backward while channeling this skill.
Level 1 Relic Gauge Cost: 65 per sec. Hold down the key to continuously attack up to 4 enemies, for 360% damage, 6 times.
While channeling this skill, damage taken from enemy attacks (including attacks that deal a fixed percentage of damage) is reduced by 60%.
This skill will end early if the Relic gauge doesn't have enough points.
Cooldown: 60 sec.

Description Fires a blast of compressed Erdas at nearby enemies.

Active Decent Holy Fountain
Master Level 25
Description Summon a Holy Fountain that restores party members' HP. Even party members with the Undead status can use it. Approach the fountain and press the up arrow key to heal.
Can't be used on a map where another party member's Holy Fountain or Decent Holy Fountain already exists.
If the Decent Holy Fountain disappears before its duration ends, a Vestige of Divinity will remain. cCan't be used on a map where another party member's Holy Fountain, Decent Holy Fountain, or Vestige of Divinity already exists.
Not affected by effects which reset cooldowns, increase recovery skill potency, or increase summon duration. Cannot be summoned near a portal.
Level 1 HP Cost: 5% of max HP, Duration: 31 sec, restores 5% HP when used, able to use 5 times total.
If it disappears before duration is up, Vestige of Divinity is created in the remaining time.
Cooldown: 89 sec
[Passive Effect - All Stats: +1]

If it disappears before duration is up, Vestige of Divinity is created in the remaining time.
Cooldown: 65 sec
[Passive Effect - All Stats: +5]
30 HP Cost: 5% of max HP, Duration: 60 sec, restores 35% HP when used, able to use 20 times total.
If it disappears before duration is up, Vestige of Divinity is created in the remaining time.
Cooldown: 60 sec

Master Level 25

Active Nova Blast
Master Level 25
Description [Ancient Force]
Consume your entire Relic Gauge to fire a bolt of obliterating energy that pierces all. The more Relic Gauge consumed, the stronger the attack will be.
Level 1 Relic Gauge Cost: 200 or more required to use the skill. Consumes all energy built up in the Relic Gauge to activate an explosion 6 times that deals 420% damage 15 times to up to 15 enemies. Invulnerable while casting.
If the consumed Relic Gauge exceeds certain thresholds (25%/50%/75%/100%), Final Damage will be increased by 25%/50%/75%/100%, respectively. Ignore Def +100%

Active Raven Tempest
Master Level 25
Description [Ancient Force]
Uses the power of the relic to call forth the true form of the Shadow Raven to wreak havoc. Using Raven Tempest with the down arrow key while Fury of the Wild is summoned activates Fury of the Wild Tempest which swirls even faster.
The summoned Shadow Raven/Fury of the Wild moves in search of enemies, and you can also press the skill key to manually change its direction.
Using Action Customization allows you to switch the Command of Raven Tempest and Fury of the Wild Tempest while Fury of the Wild is summoned.
Can only be used when Shadow Raven/Fury of the Wild is summoned. Raven Tempest and Fury of the Wild Tempest are unaffected by attack reflection.
Custom Command On/Off: Right-click
Level 1 Relic Gauge Cost: 300
Raven Tempest: Duration: 27 sec, Max Enemies Hit: 12, Damage: 420%, Number of Attacks: 5
Fury of the Wild Tempest: Duration: 10 sec, Max Enemies Hit: 12, Damage: 420%, Number of Attacks: 6
Charges the Relic Gauge by 20 when attacking
Direction Change Cooldown: 2 sec, Cooldown: 120 sec
25 Relic Gauge Cost: 300
Raven Tempest: Duration: 27 sec, Max Enemies Hit: 12, Damage: 900%, Number of Attacks: 5
Fury of the Wild Tempest: Duration: 10 sec, Max Enemies Hit: 12, Damage: 900%, Number of Attacks: 6

Direction Change Cooldown: 2 sec, Cooldown: 120 sec

Enhanced by the Burst emblem to defend a wider area than normal.

Active Relic Unbound
Master Level 25
Description [Enchant Force]
Sets up an attacking Relic by completely liberating the power of Relic. When Pathfinder's attack hits, Relic that was set up resonantes and attacks according to the emblem. Cannot be used if there is no Relic emblem.
Deluge Enhancement
Sets up Relic that rapidly shoots arrows at the enemy in front.
Burst Enhancement
Sets up Relic that projects arrows that explode when hit.
Torrent Enhancement
Sets up several Relics that simulatenously attack the enemy in a certain range.

Mastery Skills

Mastery Skills are affected by Hyper Skill passives (if applicable) and Boost Node enhancements applied to the base skill.

Active HEXA Cardinal Burst
Master Level 30
Description [Cardinal Force]
An archery technique that launches an explosive arrow of condensed energy straight ahead. The arrow will detonate when it hits an enemy or reaches its maximum range.
Required Skill: Advanced Cardinal Force Lv. 20
Level 1 MP Cost: 40, Max Enemies: 8, Damage: 671%, Attack Count: 5, when the arrow explodes.
30 MP Cost: 45, Max Enemies: 8, Damage: 990%, Attack Count: 5, when the arrow explodes.

Active HEXA Bountiful Burst
Master Level 30
Description Manifests the power stored within the relic to call forth magical arrows.
When Bountiful Burst hits periodically, the power explodes and calls forth several cursed arrows.
The magical arrows and cursed arrows chase and attack enemies in range.
These magical arrows and cursed arrows target the boss with the highest Max HP first, and are not affected by attack reflection. The cursed arrows are not affected by cooldown reset.
Level 1 When using Cardinal Deluge while the relic displays the Burst emblem, there is a 41% chance to create 2 magical arrows.
These magical arrows will chase nearby enemies for 2 sec then explode on contact, dealing 243% damage to up to 4 enemies 3 times.
When attacking the same enemy, Final Damage is decreased by 30% starting with the second explosion.
When magical arrows hit every 20 sec, 6 cursed arrows are created.
Cursed Arrows: deals 122% damage to up to 4 enemies 4 times.
30 When using Cardinal Deluge while the relic displays the Burst emblem, there is a 50% chance to create 3 magical arrows.
These magical arrows will chase nearby enemies for 2 sec then explode on contact, dealing 330% damage to up to 4 enemies 3 times.
When attacking the same enemy, Final Damage is decreased by 30% starting with the second explosion.
When magical arrows hit every 20 sec, 16 cursed arrows are created.
Cursed Arrows: deals 180% damage to up to 4 enemies 4 times.

Enhancements

Enhancements require the corresponding V Skill to be leveled to max and equipped. Final Damage bonuses from Enhancements increase linearly each level, with a jump at levels 10, 20, and 30.
